| <span data-ttu-id="ccafd-817">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccafd-817">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ccafd-818">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccafd-818">Value</span></span> |

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccafd-1613">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccafd-1613">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ccafd-1614">A classe **MS-DFSR-LocalSettings** faz parte do suporte ao serviço de replicação do DFS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccafd-1614">The **ms-DFSR-LocalSettings** class is a part of the DFS Replication service support.</span></span>
